torch.SymInt], bound_symbols: dict[Any, Any]\n):\n    \"\"\"\n    Given a list of symints/ints, this function returns a calculated expression of bound_symbols' values.\n    When we trace this \"target should be a string representing the device type. \"\n            f\"Got: {type(target).__name__}\"\n        )\n\n    def allow_cpu_device(self, node: fx.Node) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"\n torch.ops.aten.slice_scatter.default,\n        )\n\n    def is_on_target_device(self, node: fx.Node) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"\n        Returns whether a node is on the target device.\n        \"\"\"\n        node_device = self.get_node_device(node)\n        return node_device is not None and node_device.type == self.target\n\n    def is_cpu_scalar_tensor(self, node: fx.Node) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"\n        Returns whether a node is a cpu scalar tensor.\n        \"\"\"\n        device = self.get_node_device(node)\n        is_cpu = device is not None and device.type == \"cpu\"\n        ten = node.meta.get(\"val\")\n        is_scalar = isinstance(ten, torch.Tensor) and len(ten.size()) == 0\n        return is_cpu and is_scalar\n\n    def all_inputs_are_cpu_scalar_or_on_target_device(self, target device.\n\n        If this function returns False, it means that this node and all of its users\n        won't be moved into the target device.\n        \"\"\"\n        if node.target == \"output\":\n            return not self.allow_outputs\n\n        if not (\n            isinstance(node.target, torch._ops.OpOverload)\n            and node.target.namespace in (\"prims\", \"aten\")\n        ):\n            return True\n\n        if is_index_put_and_requires_h2d_sync_for_gpu_value(node):\n            return True\n\n        return False\n\n    def get_node_device(self, node: ten.device\n\n    def get_cpu_indeg_count(self, graph: fx.Graph) -> dict[fx.Node, int]:\n        \"\"\"\n        Get the number of cpu inputs to a node\n        \"\"\"\n        cpu_indeg:  target_devices = OrderedSet[torch.device]()\n        constructors = []\n        cpu_placeholders: OrderedSet[fx.Node] = OrderedSet()\n\n        for node in graph.nodes:\n            device = self.get_node_device(node)\n            if device and device.type == self.target:\n                target_devices.add(device)\n\n            if (\n                self.allow_inputs\n                and node.op == \"placeholder\"\n                and self.is_cpu_scalar_tensor(node)\n            ):\n                cpu_placeholders.add(node)\n                constructors.append(node)\n                continue\n\n            if not (\n                isinstance(node.target, torch._ops.OpOverload)\n                and node.target.namespace in (\"prims\", \"aten\")\n            ):\n             continue\n\n            constructors.append(node)\n\n        # not handling multiple target devices initially\n        if not constructors or len(target_devices) != 1:\n graph.call_function(torch.ops.aten.unsqueeze.default, (elem, 0))\n                    )\n                    last_node = unsqueezed_nodes[-1]\n            with graph.inserting_after(last_node):\n which constructors cannot be moved to gpu\n        cannot_move_to_gpu = OrderedSet[fx.Node]()\n\n        # For any node in the graph, which constructors does it have a dependency on\n        constructor_dependencies: dict[fx.Node, OrderedSet[fx.Node]] = defaultdict(\n            OrderedSet\n        )\n\n        # if a cpu node has a dependency on two different cpu constructors,\n        # then if either constructor cannot be moved to gpu, the other cannot as well.\n        # In this case any node with a dependency on one will have a dependency on the other\n        equal_constructor_sets: dict[fx.Node, OrderedSet[fx.Node]] = {\n            c: OrderedSet([c]) for c in constructors\n        }\n\n        def make_dependencies_equivalent(\n            set1: OrderedSet[fx.Node], set2: OrderedSet[fx.Node]\n        ) -> OrderedSet[fx.Node]:\n            # could use union find but not worth complexity here\n            set1.update(set2)\n            for obj in set1:\n                equal_constructor_sets[obj] = set1\n            return set1\n\n        queue: list[fx.Node] = list(constructors)\n\n        for c in queue:\n            constructor_dependencies[c].add(c)\n\n        while queue:\n            node = queue.pop()\n            dependencies = constructor_dependencies[node]\n\n            for user in node.users:\n                if self.cannot_be_moved(user):\n                    cannot_move_to_gpu.update(dependencies)\n                    break\n\n                # this node was used on a op which takes in multiple devices and output a gpu\n                # tensor. we can convert its cpu input to gpu without making further changes\n                if self.allow_cpu_device(user) and self.is_on_target_device(user):\n                    del cpu_indeg[user]\n                elif (\n                    self.allow_inputs\n                    and self.all_inputs_are_cpu_scalar_or_on_target_device(user)\n                ):\n                    # _boundaries_helper(tb: TensorBox) -> tuple[str, sympy.Expr, sympy.Expr, sympy.Expr]:\n    # Calculate the maximum offset for the boundaries tensor\n    # For a strided tensor, this is sum((size[i] - 1) * stride[i]) + stride[-1]\n    # This ensures the mask check in bucketize_binary_search works correctly\n    # for both contiguous and non-contiguous tensors.\n    size = tb.get_size()\n    stride = tb.get_stride()\n    max_offset = sum((s - 1) * st for s, st in zip(size, stride)) + stride[-1]\n    return (\n        tb.get_name(),\n        size[-1],\n        max_offset,\n        stride[-1],\n    )\n\n\ndef _sorter_helper(tb: TensorBox) -> tuple[str, sympy.Expr]:\n    return tb.get_name(), tb.get_stride()[-1]\n\n\n@register_lowering(aten.searchsorted.Tensor, type_promotion_kind=None)\ndef searchsorted(\n    sorted_sequence: TensorBox,\n    self: TensorBox,\n    *,\n    out_int32: bool = False,\n    right: bool = False,\n    side: Optional[str] = None,\n    sorter: Optional[TensorBox] = None,\n) -> Union[TensorBox, ShapeAsConstantBuffer]:\n    validate_bucketize = lambda tb: V.graph.has_feature(  # noqa: E731\n        tb, BackendFeature.BUCKETIZE\n    )\n    if (\n        not validate_bucketize(sorted_sequence)\n        or not validate_bucketize(self)\n        or (sorter is not None and not validate_bucketize(sorter))\n    ):\n        return fallback_handler(aten.searchsorted.Tensor, add_to_fallback_set=False)(\n            sorted_sequence,\n            self,\n            out_int32=out_int32,\n            right=right,\n            side=side,\n            sorter=sorter,\n        )\n\n    # If side is present, override the value of right if needed.  This assumes that\n    # validation of the two options being non-contradictory is already done by the\n    # searchsorted meta-function.\n    if side is not None and side == \"right\":\n        right = True\n\n    index_dtype = torch.int32 if out_int32 else torch.int64\n    values_loader = self.make_loader()\n\n    # The entire sorted_sequence tensor needs to be used by ops.bucketize, so we need to\n    # realize it into global memory; or in other words, we can't guarantee that\n    # sorted_sequence.get_name() (used below) will exist unless we call\n    # sorted_sequence.realize().\n    sorted_sequence.realize()\n\n    if sorter is not None:\n        sorter.realize()\n\n    if len(sorted_sequence.get_size()) == 1:\n\n        def inner_fn(idx):\n            val = values_loader(idx)\n            return ops.bucketize(\n                val,\n                _boundaries_helper(sorted_sequence),\n                0,\n                index_dtype,\n                right,\n                sorter=None if sorter is None else _sorter_helper(sorter),\n                sorter_indices=None if sorter is None else 0,\n            )\n\n    else:\n\n        def inner_fn(idx):\n            val = values_loader(idx)\n\n            # Get index to the beginning of the sorted sequence within a flattened\n            # version of the array.\n            def get_flattened_index(tb: TensorBox):\n                strides = tb.get_stride()\n                return ops.index_expr(\n                    functools.reduce(\n                        operator.add, (s * i for s, i in zip(strides[:-1], idx[:-1]))\n                    ),\n                    index_dtype,\n                )\n\n            return ops.bucketize(\n                val,\n                _boundaries_helper(sorted_sequence),\n                get_flattened_index(sorted_sequence),\n                index_dtype,\n                right,\n                sorter=None if sorter is None else _sorter_helper(sorter),\n                sorter_indices=None if sorter is None else get_flattened_index(sorter),\n            )\n\n    device = self.get_device()\n    result = Pointwise.create(\n        device=device,\n        dtype=index_dtype,\n        inner_fn=inner_fn,\n        ranges=self.shape,\n    )\n    # see [NOTE: inductor bucketize realize]\n    result.realize()\n\n    return result\n\n\n@register_lowering(\n    aten.bucketize, type_promotion_kind=ELEMENTWISE_TYPE_PROMOTION_KIND.NO_OPMATH\n)\ndef bucketize(\n    input: TensorBox,\n    boundaries: TensorBox,\n    *,\n    out_int32: bool = False,\n    right: bool = False,\n):\n    assert len(boundaries.get_size()) == 1\n\n    if not (\n        V.graph.has_feature(input, BackendFeature.BUCKETIZE)\n        and V.graph.has_feature(boundaries, BackendFeature.BUCKETIZE)\n    ):\n        return fallback_handler(aten.bucketize.Tensor, add_to_fallback_set=False)(\n            input, boundaries, out_int32=out_int32, right=right\n        )\n\n    # The entire boundaries tensor needs to be used by ops.bucketize, so we\n    # need to realize it into global memory; or in other words, we can't\n    # guarantee that boundaries.get_name() (used below) will exist unless\n    # we call boundaries.realize().\n    boundaries.realize()\n    device = input.get_device()\n    input_loader = input.make_loader()\n\n    index_dtype = torch.int32 if out_int32 else torch.int64\n\n    def inner_fn(index):\n        val = input_loader(index)\n        indices = ops.bucketize(\n            val,\n            _boundaries_helper(boundaries),\n            0,\n            index_dtype,\n            right,\n        )\n\n        return indices\n\n    result = Pointwise.create(\n        device=device,\n        dtype=index_dtype,\n        inner_fn=inner_fn,\n        ranges=input.get_size(),\n    )\n\n    # [NOTE: inductor bucketize realize]\n    # bucketize_binary_search is relatively expensive, so we don't want to re-compute\n    # it unnecessarily. If we run bucketize() and then broadcast the result, we don't\n    # want this to be fused into a large number of duplicate bucketize() computations\n    # for each of the elements in the result.\n    #\n    # If no broadcasting occurs, fusions can still occur in scheduler.py\n    result.realize()\n\n    return result\n\n\ndef require_dense(_, *args, **kwargs):\n    args, kwargs = def apply_constraint(arg, fx_arg):\n        if isinstance(arg, ir.IRNode):\n            stride_order = ir.get_stride_order(\n                fx_arg.meta[\"val\"].stride(), V.graph.sizevars.shape_env\n            )\n            return ir.ExternKernel.require_stride_order(arg, stride_order)\n        if isinstance(arg, dict):\n            return {key: apply_constraint(arg[key], fx_arg[key]) for key in in kwargs.items()}\n    return args, kwargs\n\n\ndef sdpa_constraint(fx_node, *args, **kwargs):\n    # sdpa requires dense last dimension]\n\n    def apply_constraint(idx, arg, fx_arg):\n        if not isinstance(arg, ir.IRNode):\n            return arg\n\n        meta_val = fx_arg.meta[\"val\"]\n        meta_stride_expr = [\n            s.node.expr if isinstance(s, torch.SymInt) else s for s in meta_val.stride()\n        ]\n        shape_env = V.graph.sizevars.shape_env\n        stride_order = ir.get_stride_order(meta_val.stride(), shape_env)\n\n        if stride_order and stride_order[-1] != 0:\n            # contiguous stride order\n            stride_order = list(reversed(range(len(arg.get_size()))))\n\n        if (\n            fx_node.target\n            == aten._scaled_dot_product_efficient_attention_backward.default\n            and idx in (0, 5)\n        ):\n            assert len(stride_order) == 4\n            # The 0 and 5th arguments for aten._scaled_dot_product_efficient_attention_backward.default\n            # are for out and gradient_out. They have to be in\n            # (3, 1, 2, 0) stride order. Otherwise the kernel will crash.\n            # Check https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/issues/138772\n            stride_order = (3, 1, 2, 0)\n\n        if not meta_val.is_cuda:\n            return ir.ExternKernel.require_stride_order(arg, stride_order)\n\n        # This is the minimum alignment required by SDPA kernels for attention_bias.\n        # This value can be found in pytorch/aten/src/ATen/native/transformers/attention.cpp preprocess_mask\n        ALIGNMENT = 8\n\n        # effn_attn_fwd does requires dense last dim, not just alignment\n        effn_attn_fwd_bias = (\n            fx_node.target\n            == torch.ops.aten._scaled_dot_product_efficient_attention.default\n            and idx == 3\n        )\n\n        assert isinstance(arg, TensorBox)\n        if len(arg.get_size()) not in (3, 4):\n            return arg\n\n        is_aligned_tensor = ir.is_aligned_realized_tensor(arg, ALIGNMENT)\n        if is_aligned_tensor:\n            return ir.try_match_insignificant_strides(\n                ir.ExternKernel.realize_input(arg), meta_stride_expr\n            )\n\n        if (\n            isinstance(arg, IRNode)\n            and arg.maybe_get_stride() is not None\n            and is_aligned_tensor\n        ):\n            return ir.try_match_insignificant_strides(\n                ir.ExternKernel.realize_input(arg), meta_stride_expr\n            )\n\n        if effn_attn_fwd_bias:\n            out_size = list(arg.get_size())\n\n            expanded_dims = []\n            # We require a dense last dimension, but the other strides\n            # can be expanded, which results in a smaller tensor\n            maybe_stride = arg.maybe_get_stride()\n            for i in range(len(arg.get_size()) - 1):\n                if V.graph.sizevars.statically_known_equals(meta_stride_expr[i], 0) or (\n                    maybe_stride is not None\n                    and V.graph.sizevars.statically_known_equals(maybe_stride[i], 0)\n                ):\n                    expanded_dims.append(i)\n\n            # Now, pad strides to alignment\n            out_strides = [-1] * len(out_size)\n            out_strides[-1] = 1\n            stride = 1\n            for i in range(len(out_size) - 2, -1, -1):\n                if out_strides[i + 1] != 0:\n                    stride = stride * out_size[i + 1]\n\n                # the expanded dims still need to be aligned, if they are,\n                # we can make them expanded by setting the stride equal to 0\n                if i in expanded_dims:\n                    if V.graph.sizevars.statically_known_equals(\n                        out_strides[i + 1] % ALIGNMENT, 0\n                    ):\n                        out_strides[i] = 0\n                        continue\n\n                if not V.graph.sizevars.statically_known_equals(stride % ALIGNMENT, 0):\n                    stride = ceildiv(stride, ALIGNMENT) * ALIGNMENT\n\n                out_strides[i] = stride\n\n            return ir.ExternKernel.require_exact_strides(arg, out_strides)\n\n        if is_aligned_tensor:\n            return ir.try_match_insignificant_strides(\n                ir.ExternKernel.realize_input(arg), meta_stride_expr\n            )\n\n        if (\n            isinstance(arg, IRNode)\n            and arg.maybe_get_stride() is not None\n            and is_aligned_tensor\n        ):\n            return ir.try_match_insignificant_strides(\n                ir.ExternKernel.realize_input(arg), meta_stride_expr\n            )\n\n        def is_aligned(x):\n            return V.graph.sizevars.guard_or_false(\n                sympy.Eq(Mod(x.get_size()[-1], ALIGNMENT), 0)\n            )\n\n        if isinstance(arg.data, ir.BaseView):\n            if not is_aligned(arg):\n                if is_aligned(arg.unwrap_view()):\n                    return ir.try_match_insignificant_strides(\n                        ir.ExternKernel.realize_input(arg), meta_stride_expr\n                    )\n\n        return ir.ExternKernel.require_stride_order(arg, stride_order)\n\n    args = tuple(\n        apply_constraint(idx, arg, fx_arg)\n        for idx, (arg, fx_arg) in enumerate(zip(args, fx_node.args))\n    )\n    kwargs = {k: apply_constraint(-1, v, fx_node.kwargs[k]) for k, v in kwargs.items()}\n    return args, kwargs\n\n\n# WIP\nmake_fallback(aten._adaptive_avg_pool3d)  # _local_scalar_dense(data):\n    # This is interesting!  Most lowerings return tensors, so you can just\n    # return the buffer you allocated and it will get used (or not used, if\n    # it's dead.)  But _local_scalar_dense (aka item) returns an int,\n    # not a Tensor, so you would have a type mismatch if you return a buffer;\n    # we are obligated to return a sympy expression instead.  However,\n    # we need to actually codegen the .item() call somehow.  We do this\n    # by registering a faux buffer for the DynamicScalar IR node, which is\n    # solely responsible for generating this .item().  The buffer is\n    # not used for anything (notice we discard it); at codegen time,\n    # the \"buffer\" just gets assigned None.\n    unbacked_bindings = resolve_unbacked_bindings(\n        V.graph.sizevars.shape_env, V.graph.current_node.meta[\"unbacked_bindings\"]\n    )\n    assert unbacked_bindings is not None\n    assert len(unbacked_bindings) == 1, unbacked_bindings\n    # NB: Have to be very careful here.  V.graph.current_node.meta[\"val\"]\n    # seemingly also contains a symbol which you want to do binding for,\n    # but it actually isn't.  In particular, if we have later performed\n    # a deferred runtime assert saying that u0 == s0, you will actually\n    # see s0 from expr!  This is bad because we need to actually generate\n    # the assert that says u0 == s0, so we need to know where to get u0\n    # from (this call).  In particular, we must use unbacked_bindings, which\n    # is guaranteed to have the original, unreplaced symbol in question.\n    #\n    # NB2: Another thing we have to be very careful about are symbol bindings\n    # that require nontrivial refinement, e.g., when you have a binding site\n    # x: Sym(u0 * 4) = y.item().  Here, the code generation must do a division\n    # in order to appropriately bind u0.  This is communicated via the keypath\n    # in unbacked_bindings, and we need to hold onto it in order to generate\n    # code appropriately for this case.\n    binding_sym, keypath = next(iter(unbacked_bindings.items()))\n    buffer = ir.DynamicScalar(binding_sym, keypath, data)\n    buffer.name = V.graph.register_buffer(buffer)\n    V.graph.register_operation(buffer)\n    # NB: the replaced expr is OK to use directly downstream, we want\n    # simplifications in this case!\n    val = V.graph.current_node.meta[\"val\"]\n    if isinstance(val, (torch.SymInt, torch.SymFloat, torch.SymBool)):\n        return val.node.expr\n    else:\n        return sympy.sympify(val)\n\n\n@register_lowering(aten._assert_scalar)\ndef _assert_scalar(data, msg):\n    # In this case, the tensor index is pulled to the beginning.\n    #\n    # Suppose a = torch.arange(3 * 4 * 5 * 6 * 7).view(3, 4, 5, 6, 7)\n    #         x = torch.tensor[1,2]\n    # Then, a[:,x,:,x,:] will have shape 2,3,5,7 as due to x,:,x then 2 will\n    # be pulled to the front.\n    non_consecutive_tensors = False\n    for previous, current in itertools.pairwise(tensor_indices):\n        if float\n) -> Optional[TensorBox]:\n    \"\"\"\n    This optimization changes the semantics of padding from 'clone'\n    style to 'view' style.\n\n    Thanks to functionalization, this change can still maintain numerical\n    correctness.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def _padding_can_be_fused():\n        \"\"\"\n        Conservatively check if padding can be fused with downstream op.\n        1. if the downstream op is a sum, then there is little benefit to\n           do inplace padding\n        2. if the downstream op is a matmul, doing inplace padding can\n           save membw.\n        \"\"\"\n        current_node = V.graph.current_node\n        if current_node is None:\n            return True  # be conservative\n        users = tuple(current_node.users)\n        if len(users) == 1 and users[0].target in (\n            aten.mm.default,\n            aten.addmm.default,\n        ):\n            return False\n\n        return True  # be conservative\n\n    if _padding_can_be_fused():\n        return None\n\n    # Only handle 2D case for now\n    if len(padding) != 4 or len(x.get_size()) != 2:\n        return None\n\n    # No harm to realize since we already know that\n    # the op can not be fused into the single user.\n    # It need to be realized later anyways.\n    x.realize()\n\n    # If x is a view (e.g. a SliceView), realizing it just realizing the\n    # underlying storage. x itself is still a view.\n    if (\n        not isinstance(x, ir.TensorBox)\n        or not isinstance(x.data, ir.StorageBox)\n        or not (\n            isinstance(x.data.data, ir.ComputedBuffer)\n            or (\n                config.can_inplace_pad_graph_input\n                and isinstance(x.data.data, ir.InputBuffer)\n            )\n        )\n        or not x.data.data.name\n    ):\n        return None\n    x.freeze_layout()\n\n    _, layout = ir.as_storage_and_layout(x)\n    strides = layout.stride\n    if strides[1] != 1:\n        return None\n\n    if kernel_sz[dim]\n    samples_loader = samples.make_loader()\n\n    def load(prefix, i):\n        # Handle indexing for samples tensor correctly for different input dimensions\n        # samples tensor always has shape (N, C, 2) for fractional_max_pool2d where:\n        # - N=1 for 3D inputs (C,H,W), N=batch_size for 4D inputs (N,C,H,W)\n        # - C=num_channels\n        # - 2 for the two spatial dimensions (height, width)\n        samples_shape = samples.get_size()\n\n        if len(samples_shape) == 3:  # Expected: (N, C, 2)\n            if len(prefix) == 1:\n                # 3D input case: prefix=(channel,), samples=(1, C, 2)\n                # Access: samples[0, channel, dim]\n                sample = samples_loader([0, prefix[0], ndims - 1 - dim])\n            elif len(prefix) >= 2:\n                # 4D+ input case: prefix=(batch, channel, ...), samples=(batch, C, 2)\n                # Access: samples[batch, channel, dim]\n                sample = samples_loader([prefix[0], prefix[1], ndims - 1 - dim])\n            else:\n                # Edge case - shouldn't happen for valid fractional pooling\n                sample = samples_loader([0, 0, ndims - 1 - dim])\n        else:\n            # Fallback for unexpected tensor shapes\n            sample = samples_loader([*prefix, ndims - 1 - dim])\n        i_expr = ops.index_expr(i, samples.get_dtype())\n        diff = ops.index_expr(in_sz - kernel_sz, torch.int64)\n        out_sz_expr = ops.index_expr(out_sz - 1, torch.int64)\n        alpha = ops.truediv(\n            ops.to_dtype(diff, torch.float64), ops.to_dtype(out_sz_expr, torch.float64)\n        )\n        alpha = ops.where(ops.eq(out_sz_expr, 0), 0, alpha)\n        seq_i = ops.trunc((i_expr + sample) * alpha) - ops.trunc(sample * alpha)\n        seq_i = ops.to_dtype(seq_i, torch.int64)\n        mask = ops.lt(i_expr, out_sz_expr)\n        return ops.indirect_indexing(ops.where(mask, seq_i, diff), sympy.sympify(in_sz))\n\n    return divisor_override,\n    dim,\n):\n    if not stride:\n        stride = kernel_size\n    if not padding:\n        padding = [0] * dim\n    kernel_size = pad_listlike(kernel_size, dim)\n    stride =        count_include_pad,\n            divisor_override,\n        )\n\n    def compute_pool_size_without_padding(ph, pw):\n        \"\"\"\n        This computes the scaling factor that we will divide an element\n        by when `count_include_pad=False`\n        \"\"\"\n        stride_h = ops.constant(stride[0], torch.int32)\n        stride_w = ops.constant(stride[1], torch.int32)\n        pad_h = ops.add(hstart, kernel_h),\n            ops.add(ops.index_expr(height, torch.int32), pad_h),\n        )\n        wend = ops.minimum(\n            ops.add(wstart, kernel_w),\n            ops.add(ops.index_expr(width, torch.int32), pad_w),\n        )\n        hstart = ops.maximum(hstart, ops.constant(0, torch.int32))\n        wstart = ops.maximum(wstart, ops.constant(0, torch.int32))\n      FloorDiv(h - kernel_size[0] + stride[0], stride[0]), torch.int32\n        )\n        pwstart = ops.index_expr(\n            FloorDiv(w - kernel_size[1] + stride[1], stride[1]), torch.int32\n divisor_override\n                elif count_include_pad or not had_padding:\n                    scale = kernel_size[0] * kernel_size[1]\n                else:\n                    scale =                                pooled_height,\n                                check=False,\n                            ),\n                            ops.indirect_indexing(\n                       check=False,\n                            ),\n                        ]\n                    ),\n                    scale,\n                )\n\n                mask = ops.constant(0.0, torch.float32))\n                else:\n                    gradient = ops.where(mask, ops.add(gradient, part), gradient)\n        assert gradient is not None\n        return           ceil_mode,\n            count_include_pad,\n            divisor_override,\n        )\n\n    def compute_pool_size_without_padding(pd, ph, pw):\n        stride_d, stride_h, stride_w = (ops.constant(s, torch.int32) for s in stride)\n        pad_d, pad_h, pad_w = (ops.constant(p, torch.int32) for p in padding)\n        kernel_d, kernel_h, kernel_w = (\n            ops.constant(k, torch.int32) for k in kernel_size\n        )\n\n        dstart, hstart, wstart = (\n            ops.sub(ops.mul(p, s), pad)\n            for p, s, pad in zip(\n                [pd, ph, pw], [stride_d, stride_h, stride_w], [pad_d, pad_h, pad_w]\n            )\n        )\n        dend, hend, wend = (\n            ops.minimum(\n                ops.add(start, k), ops.add(ops.index_expr(dim, torch.int32), pad)\n            )\n            for start, k, dim, pad in zip(\n                [dstart, hstart, wstart],\n                [kernel_d, kernel_h, kernel_w],\n                [depth, height, width],\n                [pad_d, pad_h, pad_w],\n            )\n        )\n        dstart, hstart, wstart = (\n            ops.maximum(start, ops.constant(0, torch.int32))\n            for start in [dstart, hstart, wstart]\n        )\n        dend, hend, wend = (\n            ops.minimum(end, ops.index_expr(dim, torch.int32))\n            for end, dim in zip([dend, hend, wend], [depth, height, width])\n        )\n        divide_factor = ops.mul(\n            ops.mul(ops.sub(dend, dstart), ops.sub(hend, hstart)), ops.sub(wend, wstart)\n        )\n        return divide_factor\n\n    def fn(idx):\n        *prefix, d, h, w = idx\n        d, h, w = (v + pad for v, pad in zip([d, h, w], padding))\n\n        pdstart, phstart, pwstart = (\n            ops.index_expr(FloorDiv(v - k + s, s), torch.int32)\n            for v, k, s in zip([d, h, w], kernel_size, stride)\n        )\n\n        pdend, phend, pwend = (\n            ops.index_expr(FloorDiv(v, s) + 1, torch.int32)\n            for v, s in zip([d, h, w], stride)\n        )\n\n        pdstart, phstart, pwstart = (\n            ops.maximum(pstart, ops.constant(0, torch.int32))\n            for pstart in [pdstart, phstart, pwstart]\n        )\n        pdend, phend, pwend = (\n            ops.minimum(pend, ops.index_expr(pooled_dim, torch.int32))\n            for pend, pooled_dim in zip(\n                [pdend, phend, pwend], [pooled_depth, pooled_height, pooled_width]\n            )\n        )\n\n        gradient = None\n        # Iterate over the 3D region to accumulate gradients\n        for pd_ in range(d_window_size):\n            for ph_ in range(h_window_size):\n                for pw_ in range(w_window_size):\n                    pd, ph, pw = (\n                        ops.add(pstart, ops.constant(p_, torch.int32))\n                        for pstart, p_ in zip(\n                            [pdstart, phstart, pwstart], [pd_, ph_, pw_]\n                        )\n                    )\n\n                    if divisor_override is not None:\n                        scale = divisor_override\n                    elif count_include_pad or not had_padding:\n                        scale = kernel_size[0] * kernel_size[1] * kernel_size[2]\n                    else:\n                        scale = compute_pool_size_without_padding(pd, ph, pw)\n\n                    part = ops.truediv(\n                        grad_loader(\n                            [\n                                *prefix,\n                                ops.indirect_indexing(\n                                    ops.minimum(\n                                        pd, ops.sub(pdend, ops.constant(1, torch.int32))\n                                    ),\n                                    pooled_depth,\n                                    check=False,\n                                ),\n                                ops.indirect_indexing(\n                                    ops.minimum(\n                                        ph, ops.sub(phend, ops.constant(1, torch.int32))\n                                    ),\n                                    pooled_height,\n                                    check=False,\n                                ),\n                                ops.indirect_indexing(\n                                    ops.minimum(\n                                        pw, ops.sub(pwend, ops.constant(1, torch.int32))\n                                    ),\n                                    pooled_width,\n                 gradient = ops.where(\n                            mask, part, ops.constant(0.0, torch.float32)\n                        )\n                    else:\n                        gradient dtype=dtype,\n        inner_fn=fn,\n        ranges=new_size,\n    )\n    return rv\n\n\ndef _validate_reduction_axis(x, axis):\n    size = x.get_size()\n    if isinstance(axis, int):\n        axis = def loader(index, reduction_index):\n        assert len(reduction_index) == len(reduced_idx)\n        if keepdims:\n            assert len(index) == len(size)\n            index = [index[i] for i in        raise RuntimeError(f\"unsupported memory format: {memory_format}\")\n\n    if memory_format == torch.channels_last:\n        assert len(size) == 4\n    if memory_format == ):\n        if is_float_dtype(dtype):\n            uninitialized_val = float(\"nan\")\n        elif is_integer_dtype(dtype):\n            uninitialized_val = torch.iinfo(dtype).max\n        else:\n executing them through V.graph.\n\n    This is a common pattern for executing a subgraph's nodes:\n    - Placeholder nodes are mapped to the provided args\n    - Output nodes return their result\n    - Other nodes are executed via V.graph.run_node\n\n    \"\"\"\n    output = None\n\n    for i, node in enumerate(graph_module.graph.nodes):\n        if node.op == \"placeholder\":\n            assert node not in V.graph.env\n            V.graph.env[node] = args[i]\n            continue\n        elif node.op == \"output\":\n            output_args, kwargs = During lowering:\n    1. Realize all additional dependencies to ensure they're computed\n    2. Execute the target operation normally\n    3. Track the dependencies for the scheduler\n    \"\"\"\n    # Realize all additional dependencies\n    dep_names = []\n    for dep in additional_deps:\n        if not isinstance(dep, IRNode):\n            continue\n\n        dep.realize()\n        dep_names.append(dep.get_name())\n\n    original_args = V.graph.current_node.args\n    arg_offset = 2  # torch.types._Number) if include_non_tensor_args else (Tensor,)\n        )  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n        flat_args = [\n            x\n            for x in pytree.arg_tree_leaves(*args, **kwargs)\n            if isinstance(x, allowed_types)\n        ]\n        computation_dtype, result_dtype = utils.elementwise_dtypes(\n            *flat_args, type_promotion_kind=type_promotion\n        )\n\n        # TODO: pretty sure this is not quite right\n        def increase_prec(x):\n            if isinstance(x, Tensor):\n                return x.to(computation_dtype)\n            else:\n                return x\n\n        def decrease_prec(x):\n            if isinstance(x, Tensor):\n                return x.to(result_dtype)\n            else:\n                return x\n\n        r = f(*tree_map(increase_prec, args), **tree_map(increase_prec, kwargs))\n        if compute_dtype_only:\n            return r\n        else:\n            return tree_map(decrease_prec, r)\n\n    return inner\n\n\ncompute_only_pw_cast_for_opmath = partial(\n    type_casts,\n    type_promotion=utils.ELEMENTWISE_TYPE_PROMOTION_KIND.DEFAULT,\n    compute_dtype_only=True,\n)\npw_cast_for_opmath = M_SQRT2 = 1.41421356237309504880\n    M_SQRT1_2 = 0.70710678118654752440\n    M_2_SQRTPI = 1.12837916709551257390\n    if approximate == \"tanh\":\n        kBeta = M_SQRT2 * M_2_SQRTPI * 0.5\n    right = 1 + tanh_inner\n\n        left_derivative = 0.5 * right\n\n        tanh_derivative = 1 - tanh_inner * tanh_inner\n        inner_derivative = kBeta * (1 + 3 * kKappa * x_sq)\n        right_derivative = left * tanh_derivative * inner_derivative\n\n        return grad * (left_derivative + right_derivative)\n    else:\n        kAlpha = M_SQRT1_2\n        kBeta = M_2_SQRTPI * M_SQRT1_2 * 0.5\n        cdf = 0.5 * (1 + torch.erf(self * kAlpha))\n        pdf = kBeta * torch.exp(self * self * -0.5)\n        return grad * (cdf + self * pdf)\n\n\n@register_decomposition(aten.mish_backward)\n@pw_cast_for_opmath\ndef mish_backward(grad_output: Tensor, input: Tensor):\n    input_tanh_softplus = torch.tanh(F.softplus(input))\n x1.pow(2).sum(-1, True)\n    x1_pad = torch.ones_like(x1_norm, memory_format=torch.contiguous_format)\n    x2_norm = x2.pow(2).sum(-1, True)\n    x2_pad = torch.ones_like(x2_norm, memory_format=torch.contiguous_format)\n    x1_ = torch.cat([x1.mul(-2), x1_norm, x1_pad], -1)\n    x2_ = torch.cat([x2, x2_pad, x2_norm], -1)\n    result = x1_.matmul(x2_.mT)\n    return result.clamp_min(0).sqrt()\n\n\n@register_decomposition(aten.slice_backward)\n@out_wrapper()\ndef slice_backward(\n    grad_output: Tensor,\n    input_sizes: list[int],\n    dim: int,\n    start: int,\n    end: int,\n    step: int,\n):\n    grad_input = grad_output.new_zeros(input_sizes)\n    return torch.slice_scatter(grad_input, grad_output, dim, start, end, step)\n\n\n@register_decomposition(aten.slice.Tensor)\ndef slice_forward(\n    # Tensor(a) self, int dim=0, SymInt? start=None, SymInt? end=None, SymInt step=1\n    self: Tensor,\n    dim: int = 0,\n    start: Optional[int] = None,\n    end: Optional[int] = None,\n    step: int = 1,\n):\n    from torch.fx.experimental.symbolic_shapes import statically_known_true\n\n    ndim = self.dim()\n    if ndim == 0:\n        raise RuntimeError(\"slice() cannot be applied to a 0-dim tensor.\")\n    dim = utils.canonicalize_dim(self.dim(), dim)\n    sizes = list(self.size())\n    strides = list(self.stride())\n\n    if step <= 0:\n        raise RuntimeError(\"slice step must be positive\")\n\n    start_val = start if start is not None else 0\n    end_val = end if end is not None else sys.maxsize  # 2^63 - 1\n\n    if start_val < 0:\n        start_val += sizes[dim]\n\n    if end_val < 0:\n        end_val += sizes[dim]\n\n    if start_val < 0:\n        start_val = 0\n    elif start_val > sizes[dim]:\n        start_val = sizes[dim]\n\n    if statically_known_true(end_val == sys.maxsize):\n        end_val = sizes[dim]\n    elif end_val < start_val:\n        end_val = start_val\n    elif end_val > sizes[dim]:\n        end_val = sizes[dim]\n\n    storage_offset = self.storage_offset() + start_val * strides[dim]\n    len = end_val - start_val\n    sizes[dim] = (len + step - 1) // step\n    strides[dim] *= step\n\n    if self.is_quantized:\n        raise NotImplementedError(\n            \"Slice decomposition for quantized tensors aren't implemented\"\n        )\n    else:\n        return self.as_strided(sizes, strides, storage_offset)\n\n\ndef _normalize_start_end(\n    x: Tensor, dim: int, start: Optional[int], end: Optional[int]\n) -> tuple[int, int]:\n    \"\"\"\n    Normalize start and end such that both are in the range\n    [0, x.get_size()[dim]] and start <= end.\n    \"\"\"\n    dim_size = x.shape[dim]\n\n    def clamp_wrap(val, lower, upper, default) -> int:\n        if val is None:\n            return default\n        if val < 0:\n            val = val + dim_size\n        return min(max(val, lower), upper)\n\n    start = clamp_wrap(start, 0, dim_size, 0)\n    end = clamp_wrap(end, start, dim_size, dim_size)\n    return start, end\n\n\n# This is not in torch._refs because aten.index used by\n# aten._unsafe_masked_index does not have a decomposition.\n@register_decomposition(aten.slice_scatter)\n@out_wrapper()\ndef slice_scatter(\n    input: Tensor,\n    src: Tensor,\n    dim: int = 0,\n    start: Optional[int] = None,\n    end: Optional[int] = None,\n    step: int = 1,\n):\n    dim = utils.canonicalize_dim(input.ndim, dim)\n    dim_size = input.shape[dim]\n    start, end = _normalize_start_end(input, dim, start, end)\n\n    src_size = list(input.shape)\n    src_size[dim] = (end - start + (step - 1)) // step\n    src = src.expand(src_size)\n\n    if start == 0 and end == dim_size and step == 1:\n        return src.clone()\n\n    indices: list[Optional[Tensor]] = [None] * input.dim()\n    idx = torch.arange(dim_size, device=input.device)\n    indices[dim] = (idx - start) // step\n\n    mask = torch.ones(dim_size, device=input.device, dtype=torch.bool)\n    if start != 0:\n        mask = torch.logical_and(mask, idx >= start)\n\n    if end != dim_size:\n        mask = torch.logical_and(mask, idx < end)\n\n    if step != 1:\n        mask = torch.logical_and(mask, (idx - start) % step == 0)\n\n    mask_shape = [1] * input.dim()\n    mask_shape[dim] = -1\n    mask = mask.view(mask_shape)\n    return aten.where(mask, aten._unsafe_masked_index(src, mask, indices, 0), input)\n\n\n@register_decomposition(aten.select_backward)\n@out_wrapper()\ndef select_backward(grad_output: Tensor, input_sizes: list[int], dim: int, index: int):\n    grad_input = grad_output.new_zeros(input_sizes)\n    return torch.select_scatter(grad_input, grad_output, dim, index)\n\n\n@register_decomposition(aten.diagonal_backward)\n@out_wrapper()\ndef diagonal_backward(\n    grad_output: Tensor, input_sizes: list[int], offset: int, dim1: int, dim2: int\n):\n    grad_input = grad_output.new_zeros(input_sizes)\n    return torch.diagonal_scatter(grad_input, grad_output, offset, dim1, dim2)\n\n\ndef _cast_grad_to_input_dtype(\n    grad_output: Tensor, grad_input: Tensor, input_dtype: torch.dtype\n):\n    if grad_output.dtype != input_dtype:\n        grad_input = grad_input.to(input_dtype)\n    return grad_input\n\n\n@register_decomposition(aten._softmax_backward_data)\n@out_wrapper(\"grad_input\")\n@compute_only_pw_cast_for_opmath\ndef _softmax_backward_data(\n    grad_output: Tensor, output: Tensor, dim: int, input_dtype: torch.dtype\n):\n    new_grad_output = grad_output * output\n    grad_input = new_grad_output - output * torch.sum(\n        new_grad_output, dim=dim, keepdim=True\n    )\n\n    # CPU kernel doesn't respect input_dtype, but following check doesn't work for meta tensor\n    # if grad_output.device == torch.device(\"cpu\"):\n    #     return grad_input.contiguous()\n\n    return _cast_grad_to_input_dtype(grad_output, grad_input, input_dtype).contiguous()\n\n\n@register_decomposition(aten._log_softmax_backward_data)\n@out_wrapper()\n@compute_only_pw_cast_for_opmath\ndef _log_softmax_backward_data(\n    grad_output: Tensor, output: Tensor, dim: int, input_dtype: torch.dtype\n):\n    grad_input = grad_output - torch.exp(output) * torch.sum(\n        grad_output, dim=dim, keepdim=True\n    )\n    return _cast_grad_to_input_dtype(grad_output, grad_input, input_dtype)\n\n\ndef _im2col_col2im_indices_along_dim(\n    input_d, kernel_d, dilation_d, padding_d, stride_d, device\n):\n    \"\"\"Utility function to implement im2col and col2im\"\"\"\n    blocks_d = input_d + padding_d * 2 - dilation_d * (kernel_d - 1)\n\n    arange_kw = partial(torch.arange, dtype=torch.int64, device=device)\n\n    # Stride kernel over input and find starting indices along dim d\n    blocks_d_indices = arange_kw(0, blocks_d, stride_d).unsqueeze(0)\n\n    # Apply dilation on kernel and find its indices along dim d\n    kernel_grid = arange_kw(0, kernel_d * dilation_d, dilation_d).unsqueeze(-1)\n\n    # Broadcast and add kernel starting positions (indices) with\n    # kernel_grid along dim d, to get block indices along dim d\n    return blocks_d_indices + kernel_grid\n\n\n@register_decomposition(aten.im2col)\n@out_wrapper()\ndef im2col(\n    input: Tensor,\n    kernel_size: list[int],\n    dilation: list[int],\n    padding: list[int],\n    stride: list[int],\n) -> Tensor:\n    torch._check(len(kernel_size) == 2, lambda: \"im2col(): only 2D kernel supported\")\n    torch._check(len(dilation) == 2, lambda: \"im2col(): only 2D dilation supported\")\n    torch._check(len(padding) == 2, lambda: \"im2col(): only 2D padding supported\")\n    torch._check(len(stride) == 2, lambda: \"im2col(): only 2D stride supported\")\n\n    def check_positive(param, param_name, strict=True):\n        cond = all(p > 0 for p in param) if strict else all(p >= 0 for p in param)\n        torch._check(\n            cond, lambda: f\"{param_name} should be greater than zero, but got {param}\"\n        )\n\n    check_positive(kernel_size, \"kernel_size\")\n    check_positive(dilation, \"dilation\")\n    check_positive(dilation, \"padding\", strict=False)\n    check_positive(stride, \"stride\")\n\n    shape = input.shape\n    ndim = len(shape)\n    torch._check(\n        ndim in (3, 4) and all(d != 0 for d in shape[-3:]),\n        lambda: \"Expected 3D or 4D (batch mode) tensor for input with possible 0 batch size \"\n        f\"and non-zero dimensions, but got: {tuple(shape)}\",\n    )\n    output_size = tuple(\n        1 + (out + 2 * pad - dil * (ker - 1) - 1) // st\n        for out, pad, dil, ker, st in zip(\n            shape[-2:], padding, dilation, kernel_size, stride\n        )\n    )\n    torch._check(\n        all(c > 0 for c in output_size),\n        lambda: f\"Given an input with spatial size {tuple(shape[-2:])}, \"\n        f\"kernel_size={kernel_size}, dilation={dilation}, \"\n        f\"padding={padding}, stride={stride}, \"\n        \"the calculated shape of the array of sliding blocks \"\n        f\"is {output_size}, but its components must be at least one.\",\n    )\n    batched_input = ndim == 4\n    if not batched_input:\n        input = input.unsqueeze(0)\n\n    batch_dim, channel_dim, input_h, input_w = input.shape\n\n    stride_h, stride_w = stride\n dilation_h, padding_h, stride_h, input.device\n    )\n    blocks_col_indices = _im2col_col2im_indices_along_dim(\n        input_w, kernel_w, dilation_w, padding_w, stride_w, input.device\n    )\n\n    # Note that F.pad takes (padding_left, padding_right, padding_top, padding_bottom)\n    # ugh\n    padded_input = F.pad(input, (padding_w, padding_w, padding_h, padding_h))\n\n    blocks_row_indices = blocks_row_indices.unsqueeze(-1).unsqueeze(-1)\n    output = padded_input[:, :, blocks_row_indices, blocks_col_indices]\n    output = output.permute(0, 1, 2, 4, 3, 5)\n    num_blocks_row = blocks_row_indices.size(1)\n    num_blocks_col = blocks_col_indices.size(1)\n    output = output.reshape(\n        batch_dim, channel_dim * kernel_h * kernel_w, num_blocks_row * num_blocks_col\n    )\n\n    if not batched_input:\n        output = output.squeeze(0)\n    return output\n\n\n@register_decomposition(aten.col2im)\n@out_wrapper()\n@pw_cast_for_opmath\ndef col2im(\n    input: Tensor,\n    output_size: list[int],\n    kernel_size: list[int],\n    dilation: list[int],\n    padding: list[int],\n    stride: list[int],\n) -> Tensor:\n    torch._check(len(output_size) == 2, lambda: \"only 2D output_size supported\")\n    torch._check(len(kernel_size) == 2, lambda: \"only 2D kernel supported\")\n    torch._check(len(dilation) == 2, lambda: \"only 2D dilation supported\")\n    torch._check(len(padding) == 2, lambda: \"only 2D padding supported\")\n    torch._check(len(stride) == 2, lambda: \"only 2D stride supported\")\n\n    def check_positive(param, param_name, strict=True):\n        cond = all(p > 0 for p in param) if strict else all(p >= 0 for p in param)\n        torch._check(\n            cond, lambda: f\"{param_name} should be greater than zero, but got {param}\"\n        )\n\n    check_positive(kernel_size, \"kernel_size\")\n    check_positive(dilation, \"dilation\")\n    check_positive(padding, \"padding\", strict=False)\n    check_positive(stride, \"stride\")\n    check_positive(output_size, \"output_size\")\n\n    shape = input.shape\n    ndim = len(shape)\n    torch._check(\n        ndim in (2, 3) and all(d != 0 for d in shape[-2:]),\n        lambda: \"Expected 2D or 3D (batch mode) tensor for input with possible 0 batch size \"\n        f\"and non-zero dimensions, but got: {tuple(shape)}\",\n    )\n    prod_kernel_size = kernel_size[0] * kernel_size[1]\n    torch._check(\n        shape[-2] % prod_kernel_size == 0,\n        lambda: \"Expected size of input's first non-batch dimension to be divisible by the \"\n        f\"product of kernel_size, but got input.shape[-2] = {shape[-2]} and \"\n        f\"kernel_size={kernel_size}\",\n    )\n    col = [\n        1 + (out + 2 * pad - dil * (ker - 1) - 1) // st\n        for out, pad, dil, ker, st in zip(\n            output_size, padding, dilation, kernel_size, stride\n        )\n    ]\n    L = col[0] * col[1]\n    torch._check(\n        shape[-1] == L,\n        lambda: f\"Given output_size={output_size}, kernel_size={kernel_size}, \"\n        f\"dilation={dilation}, padding={padding}, stride={stride}, \"\n        f\"expected input.size(-1) to be {L} but got {shape[-1]}.\",\n    )\n    torch._check(\n        L > 0,\n        lambda: f\"Given output_size={output_size}, kernel_size={kernel_size}, \"\n        f\"dilation={dilation}, padding={padding}, stride={stride}, \"\n        f\"expected input.size(-1) to be {L} but got {shape[-1]}.\",\n    )\n    batched_input = ndim == 3\n    if not batched_input:\n        input = input.unsqueeze(0)\n\n    shape = input.shape\n\n as the backwards of im2col, so we differentiate its decomposition by hand\n    input = input.reshape([shape[0], shape[1] // prod_kernel_size] + kernel_size + col)\n    input = input.permute(0, 1, 2, 4, 3, 5)\n\n    indices_row = _im2col_col2im_indices_along_dim(\n        out_h, kernel_h, dilation_h, padding_h, stride_h, input.device\n    )\n    indices_row = _unsqueeze_to_dim(indices_row, 4)\n    indices_col = _im2col_col2im_indices_along_dim(\n        out_w, kernel_w, dilation_w, padding_w, stride_w, input.device\n    )\n\n    output_padded_size = [o + 2 * p for o, p in zip(output_size, padding)]\n    output = input.new_zeros(\n        [shape[0], shape[1] // prod(kernel_size)] + output_padded_size\n    )\n    idx = (None, None, indices_row, indices_col)\n    output = aten._unsafe_index_put(output, idx, input, accumulate=True)\n    output = F.pad(output, (-padding_w, -padding_w, -padding_h, -padding_h))\n\n    if not batched_input:\n        output = output.squeeze(0)\n    return output\n\n\n@register_decomposition(aten.native_dropout_backward)\n@out_wrapper()\ndef native_dropout_backward(grad_output: Tensor, mask: Tensor, scale: float):\n    # unfold_backward(\n    grad: Tensor, input_size: list[int], dimension: int, size: int, step: int\n) -> Tensor:\n    if len(input_size) == 0:\n        return torch.squeeze_copy(grad, 0)\n    dim = lo\n        return torch.where(\n            torch.logical_and(self >= lo, self <= hi),\n            grad_output / (self * (1.0 - self)),\n            0.0,\n        )\n    else:\n        return torch.where(\n            torch.logical_and(self >= 0.0, self <= 1.0),\n            grad_output / (self * (1.0 - Ensure that decomp also returns\n    # a contiguous tensor.\n    x = x.contiguous()\n    if half_to_float:\n        assert x.dtype == torch.half\n    computation_dtype, result_dtype = utils.elementwise_dtypes(\n        x, type_promotion_kind=utils.ELEMENTWISE_TYPE_PROMOTION_KIND.DEFAULT\n    )\n    x = x.to(computation_dtype)\n    if guard_or_false(x.numel() == 0):\n        unnormalized = torch.exp(x)\n    else:\n        x_max = torch.amax(x, dim, keepdim=True)\n        unnormalized = torch.exp(x - x_max)\n    result = unnormalized / torch.sum(unnormalized, dim, keepdim=True)\n    if not half_to_float:\n        result = result.to(result_dtype)\n    return result\n\n\n@register_decomposition(aten._log_softmax)\n@out_wrapper(exact_dtype=True)\ndef _log_softmax(x: Tensor, dim: int, half_to_float: bool):\n    from torch.fx.experimental.symbolic_shapes import guard_or_false\n\n    # eager log_softmax returns a contiguous tensor. Ensure that decomp also\n    # returns a contiguous tensor.\n    x = x.contiguous()\n    if half_to_float:\n        assert x.dtype == torch.half\n    computation_dtype, result_dtype = _pad_chunk(\n    tensors: list[Tensor],\n    dim: int,\n    num_chunks: int,\n) -> list[Tensor]:\n    padded_tensors = []\n    for tensor in tensors:\n        tensor_size = tensor.size()\n bfloat16\n@register_decomposition(aten.addmm)\n@out_wrapper(exact_dtype=True)\n@pw_cast_for_opmath\ndef addmm(self: Tensor, mat1: Tensor, mat2: Tensor, beta: int = 1, alpha: int = 1):\n    if not self.is_floating_point() and not self.is_complex():\n        beta = int(beta)\n        alpha = int(alpha)\n    out = alpha * torch.mm(mat1, mat2)\n    if beta == 0:\n        return out\n\n    # The output of aten.addmm is contiguous, we need to match this behavior in the decomposition.\n    # The original implementation 'beta * self + out' would return a strided tensor if `self` is strided.\n    # We thus use `out`, the output of torch.mm, which is always contiguous, as the first argument for addition.\n    # This is relying on TensorIterator's behavior that it takes higher precedence on the stride of first input.\n    # Alternative, we can write `(beta * self + out).contiguous()`, but it introduces another copy in some cases.\n    # This implementation is not ideal, and we should revisit this when we have a better solution.\n    return out + beta * self\n\n\n@register_decomposition(aten._addmm_activation)\n@out_wrapper()\n@pw_cast_for_opmath\ndef _addmm_activation(\n    self: self.is_cuda:\n            return aten.gelu(out, approximate=\"tanh\")\n        else:\n            return aten.gelu(out)\n    return aten.relu(out)\n\n\n@register_decomposition(aten.addmv)\n@out_wrapper(exact_dtype=True)\n@pw_cast_for_opmath\ndef addmv(self: Tensor, mat1: Tensor, vec: Tensor, beta: int = 1, alpha: int = 1):\n    if native_group_norm_backward(\n    grad_output: Tensor,\n    input: Tensor,\n    mean: Tensor,\n    rstd: Tensor,\n    gamma: Optional[Tensor],\n    N: int,\n    C: int,\n    HxW: int,\n    group: int,\n    output_mask: list[bool],\n) -> tuple[Optional[Tensor], Optional[Tensor], Optional[Tensor]]:\n    utils.check_same_device(\n        grad_output, input, mean, rstd, torch._check(\n        input.numel() == N * C * HxW,\n        lambda: f\"Expect input to have {N * C * HxW} elements\",\n    )\n    torch._check(\n        mean.shape == (N, group),\n        lambda: HxW).sum(dim=[2])\n\n    d_input: Optional[Tensor] = None\n    d_gamma: Optional[Tensor] = None\n    d_bias: Optional[Tensor] = None\n    if output_mask[0]:\n        s = 1.0 / (HxW * cpg)\n        if gamma is not None:\n            ds_val = torch.mul(ds, gamma.unsqueeze(0)).reshape(N, group, cpg).sum(2)\n            db_val = torch.mul(db, gamma.unsqueeze(0)).reshape(N, group, cpg).sum(2)\n            c1 = torch.mul(\n                rstd.unsqueeze(-1),\n                gamma.reshape(1, group, cpg),\n            )\n        else:\n            ds_val = ds.reshape(N, group, cpg).sum(2)\n            db_val = db.reshape(N, group, cpg).sum(2)\n            c1 = torch.mul(\n                rstd.unsqueeze(-1),\n                torch.ones((1, group, cpg), device=rstd.device),\n            )\n        c2 = (db_val * mean - ds_val) * rstd * rstd * rstd * s\n        c3 = -c2 * mean - db_val * rstd * s\n\n        c1 = c1.unsqueeze(-1)\n        c2 = _unsqueeze_to_dim(c2, 4)\n        c3 = _unsqueeze_to_dim(c3, 4)\n        d_input = (\n            torch.mul(grad_output.reshape(N, group, cpg, HxW), c1)\n            + torch.mul(input.reshape(N, group, cpg, HxW), c2)\n            + c3\n        )\n        d_input = d_input.reshape(input.shape).to(input.dtype)\n    if output_mask[1]:\n        d_gamma = (\n            (\n                (ds.view(N, group, cpg) - db.view(N, group, cpg) * semantics\n@register_decomposition(aten.native_layer_norm_backward.default)\ndef native_layer_norm_backward(\n    grad_out: Tensor,\n    input: Tensor,\n    normalized_shape: list[int],\n    mean: Tensor,\n    normalized_shape: list[int],\n    weight: Optional[Tensor],\n    eps: Optional[float],\n) -> tuple[Tensor, Tensor]:\n    dims_to_reduce: list[int] = []\n    for i in (torch.float32, torch.complex64):\n            eps_val = torch.finfo(torch.float32).eps\n        else:\n            eps_val = torch.finfo(torch.float64).eps\n    else:\n        eps_val = eps\n\n torch.channels_last_3d,\n    )\n\n    if not is_nested and not is_channels_last:\n        upcasted_result = upcasted_result.contiguous()\n        rqrst_input = rqrst_input.contiguous()\n\n    # Cast _fused_rms_norm_backward(\n    grad_out: Tensor,\n    input: Tensor,\n    normalized_shape: list[int],\n    rstd: Tensor,\n    weight: Optional[Tensor],\n    output_mask: list[bool],\n) -> Optional[Tensor],\n    bias: Optional[Tensor],\n    running_mean: Optional[Tensor],\n    running_var: Optional[Tensor],\n    training: bool,\n    momentum: float,\n    eps: float,\n    functional: bool,\n) -> tuple[Tensor, Tensor, Tensor, Optional[Tensor], Optional[Tensor]]:\n    reduction_dims = [0] + list(range(2, input.dim()))\n    computation_dtype = utils.get_computation_dtype(input.dtype)\n    new_running_mean = running_mean\n    new_running_var = running_var\n    if training:\n        computation_dtype = utils.get_computation_dtype(input.dtype)\n        input_acc = input.to(dtype=computation_dtype)\n        biased_var, mean = torch.var_mean(\n            input_acc, dim=reduction_dims, correction=0, keepdim=True\n        )\n        rstd = torch.rsqrt(biased_var + eps)\n\n        output = (input - mean) * rstd\n\n        save_mean = torch.squeeze(mean, reduction_dims)\n        save_rstd = torch.squeeze(rstd, reduction_dims)\n        if running_mean is not None:\n            new_running_mean = momentum * save_mean + (1 - momentum) * running_mean\n            if not functional:\n                running_mean.copy_(new_running_mean)\n        if running_var is not None:\n            n = input.numel() / input.shape[1]\n            # This doesn't strictly match eager's numerics, which accumulates var sum and then directly applies the correction\n            # But... that would require re-implementing var here, for negligible numerics gain on a tensor whose\n            # numerics probably don't matter.\n            squeezed_var = torch.squeeze(biased_var, reduction_dims)\n            unbiased_var = squeezed_var * (n / (n - 1))\n            new_running_var = momentum * unbiased_var + (1 - momentum) * running_var\n            if not functional:\n                running_var.copy_(new_running_var)\n    else:\n        assert running_mean is not None and running_var is not None\n        running_mean = running_mean.to(dtype=computation_dtype, copy=True)\n        new_running_mean = running_mean\n        running_var = running_var.to(dtype=computation_dtype, copy=True)\n        new_running_var = running_var\n        mean = running_mean\n        invstd = 1 / (torch.sqrt(running_var + eps))\n        # Very annoying inconsistency where CPU and CUDA give different shapes\n        if input.device.type != \"cpu\":\n            save_mean = running_mean\n            save_rstd = invstd\n        else:\n            save_mean = input.new_zeros((0,))\n            save_rstd = input.new_zeros((0,))\n        mean = _unsqueeze_to_dim(mean, input.dim() - 1)\n        invstd = _unsqueeze_to_dim(invstd, input.dim() - 1)\n        output = (input - mean) * invstd\n\n    if weight is not None:\n        weight = weight.flatten()\n        weight = _unsqueeze_to_dim(weight, input.dim() - 1)\n        output = output * weight\n\n    if bias is not None:\n        bias = bias.flatten()\n        bias = _unsqueeze_to_dim(bias, input.dim() - 1)\n        output = output + bias\n\n    if input.device.type == \"cpu\":\n        save_mean = save_mean.to(dtype=input.dtype)\n        save_rstd = save_rstd.to(dtype=input.dtype)\n    return (\n        output.to(dtype=input.dtype),\n        save_mean,\n        save_rstd,\n        new_running_mean,\n        new_running_var,\n    )\n\n\n@register_decomposition(aten.native_batch_norm)\n@out_wrapper(\"out\", \"save_mean\", \"save_invstd\")\ndef native_batch_norm(\n    input: Tensor,\n    weight: Optional[Tensor],\n    bias: Optional[Tensor],\n    running_mean: Optional[Tensor],\n    running_var: Optional[Tensor],\n    training: bool,\n    momentum: float,\n    eps: float,\n) -> tuple[Tensor, Tensor, Tensor]:\n    output, save_mean, save_rstd, _, _ = native_batch_norm_helper(\n        input, weight, bias, running_mean, running_var, training, momentum, eps, False\n    )\n    return output, save_mean, save_rstd\n\n\n# TODO: this decomposition is NOT here to stay. We would much prefer replacing native_batch_norm\n# with our new correctly schema'd _native_batch_norm_legit and its variants, but\n# we cannot do that immediately in the C++ because it would be input: Tensor,\n    weight: Optional[Tensor],\n    bias: Optional[Tensor],\n    running_mean: Optional[Tensor],\n    running_var: Optional[Tensor],\n    training: bool,\n    momentum: float,\n    eps: float,\n) -> tuple[Tensor, Tensor, Tensor]:\n    if running_mean is None and running_var is None:\n        return aten._native_batch_norm_legit(\n            input, weight, bias, training, momentum, Optional[Tensor],\n    running_var: Optional[Tensor],\n    save_mean: Optional[Tensor],\n    save_invstd: Optional[Tensor],\n    train: bool,\n    eps: float,\n    output_mask: list[bool],\n) -> tuple[Tensor, Optional[Tensor], Optional[Tensor]]:\n    input_dtype = input.dtype\n    if weight is not None:\n        weight_dtype = weight.dtype\n    else:\n        weight_dtype = input_dtype\n    computation_dtype = utils.get_computation_dtype(input.dtype)\n    (\n        grad_out_cast,\n        input_cast,\n        weight_cast,\n        running_mean_cast,\n        running_var_cast,\n        save_mean_cast,\n        save_invstd_cast,\n    ) = (\n        x.to(computation_dtype) if x is not None else x\n        for x in (\n            grad_out,\n            input,\n            weight,\n            running_mean,\n            running_var,\n            save_mean,\n            save_invstd,\n        )\n    )\n    input_shape = input.shape\n    input_rank = input.dim()\n    assert input_rank >= 2, \"rank of the input must be at least 2\"\n\n    axis = 1\n    num_features = prod(list(input_shape)) / input_shape[axis]\n    mean = save_mean_cast\n    invstd = save_invstd_cast\n    if train:\n        assert mean is not None and invstd is not None\n\n    else:\n        assert running_mean_cast is not None and running_var_cast is not None\n        mean = running_mean_cast\n        invstd = torch.rsqrt(running_var_cast + eps)\n\n    broadcast_mask: list[int] = [1] * input_rank\n    broadcast_mask[axis] = input_shape[axis]\n\n    reduction_axes: list[int] = []\n    for i in range(input_rank):\n        if i != axis:\n            reduction_axes.append(i)\n\n    mean = _broadcast_batch_norm_backward(mean, broadcast_mask)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n    norm = 1.0 / num_features\n    grad_output_sum = torch.sum(grad_out_cast, reduction_axes)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n    dot_p = torch.sum(grad_out_cast * (input_cast - mean), reduction_axes)  # type: ignore[operator]\n\n    grad_mean = _broadcast_batch_norm_backward(grad_output_sum * norm, broadcast_mask)\n    proj_scale = _broadcast_batch_norm_backward(\n        torch.mul(dot_p * norm, invstd * invstd),  # type: ignore[operator]\n        broadcast_mask,\n    )\n\n    if weight_cast is None:\n        grad_scale = _broadcast_batch_norm_backward(invstd, broadcast_mask) * 1.0  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n    else:\n        grad_scale = _broadcast_batch_norm_backward(\n            invstd * weight_cast, broadcast_mask\n        )\n\n    if train:\n        proj = (input_cast - mean) * proj_scale  # type: ignore[operator]\n        grad_input = ((grad_out_cast - proj) - grad_mean) * grad_scale\n    else:\n        grad_input = grad_out_cast * grad_scale\n\n    if output_mask[1]:\n        grad_weight = dot_p * invstd\n    else:\n        grad_weight = None  # \"None\" doesn't work with vjp, should use zeros for vjp\n\n    if output_mask[2]:\n        grad_bias = grad_output_sum\n    else:\n        grad_bias = None  # \"None\" doesn't work with vjp, should use zeros for vjp\n\n    return (\n        grad_input.to(input_dtype),\n        _maybe_cast(grad_weight, weight_dtype),\n        _maybe_cast(grad_bias, weight_dtype),\n    )\n\n\n# out_wrapper currently does not allow optional outputs\n@register_decomposition(aten.native_batch_norm_backward.out)\ndef native_batch_norm_backward_out(\n    grad_out: Tensor,\n    input: Tensor,\n    weight: Optional[Tensor],\n    running_mean: Optional[Tensor],\n    running_var: Optional[Tensor],\n    save_mean: adaptive_avg_pool2d(input: Tensor, output_size: tuple[int, int]):\n    # Preconditions\n    device = input.device\n    shape = input.shape\n    ndim = len(shape)\n    torch._check(\n        ndim in (3, 4),\n        lambda: f\"adaptive_avg_pool2d(): Expected 3D or 4D tensor, but got {ndim}\",\n    )\n    for d in input.shape[-2:]:\n        torch._check(\n            d != 0,\n            lambda: \"adaptive_avg_pool2d(): Expected input to have non-zero size for \"\n            f\"non-batch dimensions, but input has shape {tuple(shape)}.\",\n        )\n\n    # Optimisation (we should also do this in the kernel implementation)\n    if shape[-2] % output_size[-2] == 0 and shape[-1] % output_size[-1] == 0:\n        stride = tuple(i // o for i, o in zip(shape[-2:], output_size))\n        kernel = tuple(\n            i - (o - 1) * s for i, o, s in zip(shape[-2:], output_size, stride)\n        )\n        return torch.nn.functional.avg_pool2d(input, kernel, stride)\n\n    def start_index(a, b, c):\n        return torch.div(a * c, b, rounding_mode=\"trunc\")\n\n    def end_index(a, b, c):\n        return torch.div((a + 1) * c + b - 1, b, rounding_mode=\"trunc\")\n\n    def compute_idx(in_size, out_size):\n        orange = torch.arange(out_size, device=device, dtype=torch.int64)\n        i0 = start_index(orange, out_size, in_size)\n        # Let length = end_index - start_index, i.e. the length of the pooling kernels\n        # length.max() can be computed analytically as follows:\n        maxlength = in_size // out_size + 1\n        in_size_mod = in_size % out_size\n        # adaptive = True iff there are kernels with different lengths\n        adaptive = not (in_size_mod == 0 or out_size % in_size_mod == 0)\n        if adaptive:\n            maxlength += 1\n        elif in_size_mod == 0:\n            maxlength -= 1\n\n        range_max = torch.arange(maxlength, device=device, dtype=torch.int64)\n        idx = i0.unsqueeze(-1) + range_max\n        if adaptive:\n            # Need to clamp to avoid accessing out-of-bounds memory\n            # TODO make minimum accept scalars\n            maxval = torch.scalar_tensor(\n                in_size - 1, dtype=idx.dtype, device=idx.device\n            )\n            idx = torch.minimum(idx, maxval)\n\n            # Compute the length\n            i1 = end_index(orange, out_size, in_size)\n            length = i1 - i0\n        else:\n            length = maxlength\n        return idx, length, range_max, adaptive\n\n    # length is not None if it's constant, otherwise we'll need to compute it\n    idxh, length_h, range_max_h, adaptive_h = compute_idx(shape[-2], output_size[-2])\n    idxw, length_w, range_max_w, adaptive_w = compute_idx(shape[-1], output_size[-1])\n\n    vals = input[..., _unsqueeze_to_dim(idxh, 4), idxw]\n    # Shortcut for the simpler case\n    if not adaptive_h and not adaptive_w:\n        return torch.mean(vals, dim=(-3, -1))\n\n    def maybe_mask(vals, length, range_max, adaptive, dim):\n        if isinstance(length, IntLike):\n            return vals, length\n        else:\n            # zero-out the things we didn't really want to select\n            assert dim < 0\n            # hack\n            mask = range_max >= length.unsqueeze(-1)\n            if dim == -2:\n                mask = _unsqueeze_to_dim(mask, 4)\n            vals = torch.masked_fill(vals, mask, 0.0)\n            # Compute the length of each window\n            length = _unsqueeze_to_dim(length, -dim)\n            return vals, length\n\n    vals, length_h = maybe_mask(\n        vals, length_h, range_max_h, adaptive=adaptive_h, dim=-2\n    )\n    vals, length_w = maybe_mask(\n        vals, length_w, range_max_w, adaptive=adaptive_w, dim=-1\n    )\n\n    # We unroll the sum as we assume that the kernels are going to be small\n    ret = None\n    for i, j in product(range(vals.shape[-3]), range(vals.shape[-1])):\n        if ret is None:\n            ret = vals[..., i, :, j]\n        else:\n            ret = ret + vals[..., i, :, j]\n    return ret / (length_h * length_w)\n\n\ndef _max_unpoolnd(\n    self: TensorLike, indices: TensorLike, output_size: list[int], dim: int\n):\n    # If the input tensors self and indices came from max_pool call as\n    # required by the documentation, this operation is deterministic\n    # because that ensures that if there are two entries in `indices`\n    # tensor that are equal, the corresponding values in `self` are also\n    # equal. If this condition is not satisfied, the operation is\n    # non-deterministic as one of the different values in `self` 'wins'.\n    utils.alert_not_deterministic(f\"max_unpooling{dim}d_forward_out\")\n    nc = reduce(operator.mul, self.shape[:-dim])\n    hw = reduce(operator.mul, output_size)\n    indices_nc_shape = [1] * self.ndim\n    indices_nc_shape[:-dim] = self.shape[:-dim]\n    indices_flat = (\n        indices + aten.arange(nc, device=self.device).view(indices_nc_shape) * hw\n    ).reshape(-1)\n\n    output = self.new_zeros(list(self.shape[:-dim]) + list(output_size))\n    return aten._unsafe_index_put(\n        output.reshape(-1), [indices_flat], self.reshape(-1), accumulate=False\n    ).view(output.shape)\n\n\n@register_decomposition(aten.max_unpool2d)\n@out_wrapper()\ndef max_unpool2d(\n    self: TensorLike,\n    indices: TensorLike,\n    output_size: list[int],\n):\n torch._check(len(output_size) == spatial_dimensions, lambda: \"\")\n        return output_size\n    if scale_factors is not None:\n        # NB: this isn't necessary lol\n        torch._check(\n            output_size is None,\n            lambda: \"Must specify exactly one of output_size and scale_factors\",\n        )\n        torch._check(len(scale_factors) == spatial_dimensions, lambda: \"\")\n _upsample_nearest_exact_vec(\n    input: Tensor,\n    output_size: Optional[list[int]],\n    scale_factors: Optional[list[float]],\n) -> Tensor:\n    osize = upsample_compute_output_size(input.size(), exact=True)\n\n\ndef _compute_upsample_nearest_indices(input, output_size, scales, exact=False):\n    # For each dim in output_size, compute the set of input indices used\n    # to produce the upsampled output.\n    indices = []\n    num_spatial_dims = len(output_size)\n    offset = 0.5 if exact else 0.0\n\n    for d in range(num_spatial_dims):\n        # Math matches aten/src/ATen/native/cpu/UpSampleKernel.cpp\n        #\n        # Indices are computed as following:\n        # scale = isize / osize\n        # Case: exact=False\n        # input_index = floor(output_index * scale)\n        # Same as OpenCV INTER_NEAREST\n        #\n        # Case: exact=False\n        # index_f32 = (output_index + 0.5) * scale - 0.5\n        # input_index = round(index_f32)\n        # Same as Pillow and Scikit-Image/Scipy ndi.zoom\n        osize = output_size[d]\n        isize = input.shape[-num_spatial_dims + d]\n        scale = isize / (isize * scales[d]) if scales[d] is not None else isize / osize\n\n        output_indices = torch.arange(osize, dtype=torch.float32, device=input.device)\n        input_indices = ((output_indices + offset) * scale).to(torch.int64)\n        for _ in range(num_spatial_dims - 1 - d):\n            input_indices = input_indices.unsqueeze(-1)\n        indices.append(input_indices)\n    return indices\n\n\n@register_decomposition([aten.upsample_nearest1d.default, has_biases:\n        group_size = 4\n    elif has_projections:\n        group_size = 3\n    else:\n        group_size = 2\n\n    assert len(params) % group_size == 0, len(params)\n    return [\n        tuple(params[i : i + group_size]) for i in range(0, len(params), group_size)\n    ]\n\n\ndef params_hiddens(params, hiddens, i, bidirectional):\n    if bidirectional:\n        cur_params, cur_hidden = params[2 * i], hiddens[2 * i]\n        bidir_params, bidir_hidden = params[2 * i + 1], hiddens[2 * i + 1]\n    else:\n        cur_params, cur_hidden = params[i], hiddens[i]\n        bidir_params, last_batch_size > batch_size\n    hiddens.append(cur_hidden.narrow(0, batch_size, last_batch_size - batch_size))\n    return cur_hidden.narrow(0, 0, batch_size)\n\n\ndef update_hidden_for_packed_reverse(\n    cur_hidden, last_batch_size, batch_size, inp_hidden\n):\n    if last_batch_size == batch_size:\n        return cur_hidden\n    assert last_batch_size < batch_size\n    return torch.concat(\n        (\n            cur_hidden,\n            inp_hidden.narrow(0, last_batch_size, batch_size - last_batch_size),\n        )\n    )\n\n\ndef one_layer_rnn_data(\n    inp, hidden, params, has_biases, hidden_fn, batch_sizes, reverse=False\n):\n    ih_weight = params[0]\n    hh_weight = params[1]\n    ih_bias = params[2] if has_biases else None\n    hh_bias = params[3] if has_biases else None\n\n    step_output = []\n    hiddens: list[torch.Tensor] = []\n\n    last_batch_size = batch_sizes[-1] if reverse else batch_sizes[0]\n    cur_hidden = hidden.narrow(0, 0, last_batch_size)\n    split_inp = torch.split(inp, list(batch_sizes))\n    if reverse:\n        split_inp = split_inp[::-1]\n    for inp in split_inp:\n        i = inp.shape[0]\n\n        if last_batch_size == i:\n            pass  # don't update cur_hidden\n        # this will only happen when reverse=False, since batch sizes are sorted largest -> smallest\n        elif reverse:\n            cur_hidden = update_hidden_for_packed_reverse(\n                cur_hidden, last_batch_size, i, hidden\n            )\n        else:\n            cur_hidden = update_hidden_for_packed(\n                cur_hidden, last_batch_size, i, hiddens\n            )\n\n        cur_hidden = hidden_fn(inp, cur_hidden, ih_weight, ih_bias, hh_weight, hh_bias)\n        last_batch_size = i\n        step_output.append(cur_hidden)\n\n    if reverse:\n        step_output.reverse()\n    else:\n        hiddens.append(cur_hidden)\n        hiddens.reverse()\n\n    out = torch.cat(step_output, 0)\n    hidden_out = torch.cat(hiddens, 0) if not reverse else cur_hidden\n    return out, hidden_out\n\n\ndef rnn_cell(nonlinearity):\n    def inner(i, cur_hidden, ih_weight, ih_bias, hh_weight, hh_bias):\n        return nonlinearity(F.linear(cur_hidden, hh_weight, hh_bias) + i)\n\n    return inner\n\n\ndef rnn_cell_data(nonlinearity):\n    def inner(i, cur_hidden, ih_weight, ih_bias, hh_weight, hh_bias):\n        i = F.linear(i, ih_weight, ih_bias)\n        return nonlinearity(F.linear(cur_hidden, hh_weight, hh_bias) + i)\n\n    return inner\n\n\ndef one_layer_rnn(inp, hidden, params, has_biases, hidden_fn, reverse=False):\n    ih_weight = params[0]\n    hh_weight = params[1]\n    ih_bias = params[2] if has_biases else None\n    hh_bias = params[3] if has_biases else None\n\n    precomputed_input = F.linear(inp, ih_weight, ih_bias)\n    precomputed_input = precomputed_input.flip(0) if reverse else precomputed_input\n    cur_hidden = hidden.unsqueeze(0)\n    step_output = []\n    for i in precomputed_input:\n        cur_hidden = hidden_fn(i, cur_hidden, ih_weight, ih_bias, hh_weight, hh_bias)\n        step_output.append(cur_hidden)\n\n    if reverse:\n        step_output.reverse()\n\n    out = torch.cat(step_output, 0)\n\n    return out, cur_hidden.squeeze(0)\n\n\ndef mkldnn_one_layer_lstm(inp, hard-code them to False here\n    bidirectional = False\n    batch_first = False\n\n    train = False\n    # If batch_first, inp has been permuted in _rnn_helper. Convert to contiguous here.\n    # Same as aten/src/ATen/native/mkldnn/RNN.cpp: mkldnn_rnn: input = input.contiguous();\n    inp = inp.contiguous()\n    hx = hx.contiguous()\n    cx = batch_sizes,\n        mode,\n        hidden_size,\n        num_layers,\n        has_biases,\n        bidirectional,\n        batch_first,\n        train,\n    )\n    y, hy, cy = outputs[0], outputs[1], outputs[2]\n    return y, (hy.squeeze(0), cy.squeeze(0))\n\n\ndef _rnn_helper(\n    input,\n    hidden,\n    params,\n    has_biases,\n    num_layers,\n    dropout,\n    train,\n    bidirectional,\n    batch_first,\n    layer_fn,\n):\n    input = input.transpose(0, 1) if batch_first else input\n    final_hiddens = []\n\n    for i in range(num_layers):\n        cur_params, cur_hidden, bidir_params, bidir_hidden = params_hiddens(\n            params, hidden, i, bidirectional\n        )\n        dropout = dropout if (train and num_layers < i - 1) else 0.0\n        fwd_inp, fwd_hidden = layer_fn(input, cur_hidden, cur_params, has_biases)\n        final_hiddens.append(fwd_hidden)\n\n        if bidirectional:\n            bwd_inp, bwd_hidden = layer_fn(\n                input, bidir_hidden, bidir_params, has_biases, reverse=True\n            )\n            final_hiddens.append(bwd_hidden)\n\n        if bidirectional:\n            input = torch.cat([fwd_inp, bwd_inp], fwd_inp.dim() - 1)  # type: ignore[possibly-undefined]\n        else:\n            input = fwd_inp\n\n        if dropout != 0 and train and i < num_layers - 1:\n            input = torch.dropout(input, dropout, train=True)\n\n    input = input.transpose(0, 1) if batch_first else input\n    return input, 0)\n\n\n@register_decomposition(aten.rnn_relu.input)\n@aten.rnn_relu.input.py_impl(DispatchKey.CompositeImplicitAutograd)\n@aten.rnn_relu.input.py_impl(DispatchKey.Autograd)\ndef rnn_relu_input(\n 0)\n\n\n@register_decomposition(aten.rnn_relu.data)\n@aten.rnn_relu.data.py_impl(DispatchKey.CompositeImplicitAutograd)\n@aten.rnn_relu.data.py_impl(DispatchKey.Autograd)\ndef rnn_relu_data(\n
